## Instruction

Please find all files in the workspace that are related to the "Operating Systems Fundamentals" course and belong to Assignment 3. Based on the correspondence table between colleges and student IDs, rename these files uniformly as: Name-College-StudentID-OS-HW3. Please maintain the original capitalization and spacing of student names and colleges, and do not arbitrarily add or remove words. After completing the renaming, create a new directory called "os_hw3/" , and within this directory, place them into three new subdirectories: "C", "Rust", and "Python" respectively. Please delete all the original code files, including those outside of this course and those not related to the third assignment, after completing the organization process to keep the workspace clean.

There are more than 500 files in the workspace.

```python 
print(f"Total students in mapping: {len(student_mapping)}")

# Now let's identify files related to Operating Systems Fundamentals Assignment 3
workspace_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace"
all_files = []

for file in os.listdir(workspace_path):
    if file.endswith(('.c', '.py', '.rs')) and not file == 'CollegeNameID.xlsx':
        all_files.append(file)

print(f"Total code files: {len(all_files)}")

# Patterns to identify Operating Systems Assignment 3 files
os_patterns = [
    r'OperatingSystems.*HW3',
    r'OperatingSystems.*Assignment3',
    r'OperatingSystems.*Lab3',
    r'OS.*Assignment3',
    r'OS.*HW3',
    r'OS.*Homework3',
    r'OS.*Lab3',
    r'OS.*Project3'
]

os_hw3_files = []

for file in all_files:
    for pattern in os_patterns:
        if re.search(pattern, file, re.IGNORECASE):
            os_hw3_files.append(file)
            break

print(f"Found {len(os_hw3_files)} OS HW3 files:")
for file in sorted(os_hw3_files):
    print(f"  {file}")
```

```python 
import os
import re
import shutil
from pathlib import Path

# Refined filtering for OS HW3 files - exclude non-OS subjects
os_hw3_files_filtered = []

for file in os_hw3_files:
    # Skip files that are clearly not OS-related
    if any(subject in file for subject in ['Network', 'Database', 'Compiler', 'Algorithm', 'AI', 'SE', 'DS']):
        if not any(os_term in file for os_term in ['OperatingSystems', 'OS']):
            continue
    os_hw3_files_filtered.append(file)

print(f"Filtered OS HW3 files: {len(os_hw3_files_filtered)}")

# Now let's create the renaming mapping
rename_operations = []

for file in os_hw3_files_filtered:
    # Extract student name from filename
    name_match = None
    
    # Try different patterns to extract the name
    patterns = [
        r'^([A-Za-z]+ [A-Za-z]+)[-_]',  # "Name Surname-" or "Name Surname_"
        r'^([A-Za-z]+ [A-Za-z]+) ',     # "Name Surname "
    ]
    
    for pattern in patterns:
        match = re.match(pattern, file)
        if match:
            name_match = match.group(1)
            break
    
    if not name_match:
        print(f"Could not extract name from: {file}")
        continue
    
    # Look up student info
    if name_match in student_mapping:
        student_id, college = student_mapping[name_match]
        
        # Get file extension
        extension = file.split('.')[-1]
        
        # Create new filename: Name-College-StudentID-OS-HW3.extension
        new_filename = f"{name_match}-{college}-{student_id}-OS-HW3.{extension}"
        
        rename_operations.append((file, new_filename))
    else:
        print(f"Student not found in mapping: {name_match} (from file: {file})")

print(f"\nRename operations: {len(rename_operations)}")
for old, new in rename_operations[:10]:  # Show first 10
    print(f"  {old} -> {new}")

if len(rename_operations) > 10:
    print(f"  ... and {len(rename_operations) - 10} more")
```

```python 
student_mapping.update(se_students)
student_mapping.update(cs_sec_students)

# Get all code files
workspace_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace"
all_files = []

for file in os.listdir(workspace_path):
    if file.endswith(('.c', '.py', '.rs')) and not file == 'CollegeNameID.xlsx':
        all_files.append(file)

# Patterns to identify Operating Systems Assignment 3 files
os_patterns = [
    r'OperatingSystems.*HW3',
    r'OperatingSystems.*Assignment3',
    r'OperatingSystems.*Lab3',
    r'OS.*Assignment3',
    r'OS.*HW3',
    r'OS.*Homework3',
    r'OS.*Lab3',
    r'OS.*Project3'
]

os_hw3_files = []
for file in all_files:
    for pattern in os_patterns:
        if re.search(pattern, file, re.IGNORECASE):
            os_hw3_files.append(file)
            break

# Filter out non-OS files that might have been caught by the patterns
os_hw3_files_filtered = []
for file in os_hw3_files:
    # Skip files that are clearly not OS-related
    if any(subject in file for subject in ['Network', 'Database', 'Compiler', 'Algorithm', 'AI', 'SE', 'DS']):
        if not any(os_term in file for os_term in ['OperatingSystems', 'OS']):
            continue
    os_hw3_files_filtered.append(file)

print(f"Filtered OS HW3 files: {len(os_hw3_files_filtered)}")

# Create the renaming mapping
rename_operations = []
for file in os_hw3_files_filtered:
    # Extract student name from filename
    name_match = None
    
    # Try different patterns to extract the name
    patterns = [
        r'^([A-Za-z]+ [A-Za-z]+)[-_]',  # "Name Surname-" or "Name Surname_"
        r'^([A-Za-z]+ [A-Za-z]+) ',     # "Name Surname "
    ]
    
    for pattern in patterns:
        match = re.match(pattern, file)
        if match:
            name_match = match.group(1)
            break
    
    if not name_match:
        print(f"Could not extract name from: {file}")
        continue
    
    # Look up student info
    if name_match in student_mapping:
        student_id, college = student_mapping[name_match]
        
        # Get file extension
        extension = file.split('.')[-1]
        
        # Create new filename: Name-College-StudentID-OS-HW3.extension
        new_filename = f"{name_match}-{college}-{student_id}-OS-HW3.{extension}"
        
        rename_operations.append((file, new_filename))
    else:
        print(f"Student not found in mapping: {name_match} (from file: {file})")

print(f"\nTotal rename operations: {len(rename_operations)}")
print("\nFirst 10 rename operations:")
for i, (old, new) in enumerate(rename_operations[:10]):
    print(f"  {i+1}. {old}")
    print(f"     -> {new}")
```

<svg width="14px" height="14px" viewBox="0 0 32 32" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style={{margin: 0, padding: 0, display: 'inline-block'}}><path fillRule="evenodd" clipRule="evenodd" d="M13.0164 2C10.8193 2 9.03825 3.72453 9.03825 5.85185V8.51852H15.9235V9.25926H5.97814C3.78107 9.25926 2 10.9838 2 13.1111L2 18.8889C2 21.0162 3.78107 22.7407 5.97814 22.7407H8.27322V19.4815C8.27322 17.3542 10.0543 15.6296 12.2514 15.6296H19.5956C21.4547 15.6296 22.9617 14.1704 22.9617 12.3704V5.85185C22.9617 3.72453 21.1807 2 18.9836 2H13.0164ZM12.0984 6.74074C12.8589 6.74074 13.4754 6.14378 13.4754 5.40741C13.4754 4.67103 12.8589 4.07407 12.0984 4.07407C11.3378 4.07407 10.7213 4.67103 10.7213 5.40741C10.7213 6.14378 11.3378 6.74074 12.0984 6.74074Z" fill="#327EBD"/><path fillRule="evenodd" clipRule="evenodd" d="M18.9834 30C21.1805 30 22.9616 28.2755 22.9616 26.1482V23.4815L16.0763 23.4815L16.0763 22.7408L26.0217 22.7408C28.2188 22.7408 29.9998 21.0162 29.9998 18.8889V13.1111C29.9998 10.9838 28.2188 9.25928 26.0217 9.25928L23.7266 9.25928V12.5185C23.7266 14.6459 21.9455 16.3704 19.7485 16.3704L12.4042 16.3704C10.5451 16.3704 9.03809 17.8296 9.03809 19.6296L9.03809 26.1482C9.03809 28.2755 10.8192 30 13.0162 30H18.9834ZM19.9015 25.2593C19.1409 25.2593 18.5244 25.8562 18.5244 26.5926C18.5244 27.329 19.1409 27.9259 19.9015 27.9259C20.662 27.9259 21.2785 27.329 21.2785 26.5926C21.2785 25.8562 20.662 25.2593 19.9015 25.2593Z" fill="#FFDA4B"/></svg> `python-execute`

```python 
# Create the os_hw3 directory structure
os_hw3_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/os_hw3"
c_path = os.path.join(os_hw3_path, "C")
rust_path = os.path.join(os_hw3_path, "Rust")
python_path = os.path.join(os_hw3_path, "Python")

# Create directories
os.makedirs(c_path, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(rust_path, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(python_path, exist_ok=True)

print(f"Created directory structure:")
print(f"  {os_hw3_path}/")
print(f"    C/")
print(f"    Rust/")
print(f"    Python/")

# Perform the renaming and moving operations
successful_operations = 0
failed_operations = []

for old_filename, new_filename in rename_operations:
    try:
        old_path = os.path.join(workspace_path, old_filename)
        
        # Determine target directory based on file extension
        extension = new_filename.split('.')[-1].lower()
        if extension == 'c':
            target_dir = c_path
        elif extension == 'rs':
            target_dir = rust_path
        elif extension == 'py':
            target_dir = python_path
        else:
            print(f"Unknown extension: {extension} for file: {new_filename}")
            continue
            
        new_path = os.path.join(target_dir, new_filename)
        
        # Copy and rename the file
        shutil.copy2(old_path, new_path)
        successful_operations += 1
        
        if successful_operations <= 5:  # Show first 5 operations
            print(f"‚úì {old_filename} -> {target_dir.split('/')[-1]}/{new_filename}")
            
    except Exception as e:
        failed_operations.append((old_filename, str(e)))
        print(f"‚úó Failed to process {old_filename}: {e}")

print(f"\nSummary:")
print(f"  Successful operations: {successful_operations}")
print(f"  Failed operations: {len(failed_operations)}")

if len(failed_operations) > 0:
    print(f"  Failed files:")
    for file, error in failed_operations:
        print(f"    {file}: {error}")

# Count files in each directory
c_count = len([f for f in os.listdir(c_path) if f.endswith('.c')])
rust_count = len([f for f in os.listdir(rust_path) if f.endswith('.rs')])
python_count = len([f for f in os.listdir(python_path) if f.endswith('.py')])

print(f"\nFiles organized:")
print(f"  C directory: {c_count} files")
print(f"  Rust directory: {rust_count} files")
print(f"  Python directory: {python_count} files")
print(f"  Total: {c_count + rust_count + python_count} files")
```

```python 
import os
import shutil

# Create the os_hw3 directory structure
os_hw3_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/os_hw3"
c_path = os.path.join(os_hw3_path, "C")
rust_path = os.path.join(os_hw3_path, "Rust")
python_path = os.path.join(os_hw3_path, "Python")

# Create directories
os.makedirs(c_path, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(rust_path, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(python_path, exist_ok=True)

print(f"Created directory structure:")
print(f"  {os_hw3_path}/")
print(f"    C/")
print(f"    Rust/")
print(f"    Python/")

# Perform the renaming and moving operations
workspace_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace"
successful_operations = 0
failed_operations = []

for old_filename, new_filename in rename_operations:
    try:
        old_path = os.path.join(workspace_path, old_filename)
        
        # Determine target directory based on file extension
        extension = new_filename.split('.')[-1].lower()
        if extension == 'c':
            target_dir = c_path
        elif extension == 'rs':
            target_dir = rust_path
        elif extension == 'py':
            target_dir = python_path
        else:
            print(f"Unknown extension: {extension} for file: {new_filename}")
            continue
            
        new_path = os.path.join(target_dir, new_filename)
        
        # Copy and rename the file
        shutil.copy2(old_path, new_path)
        successful_operations += 1
        
        if successful_operations <= 5:  # Show first 5 operations
            print(f"‚úì {old_filename} -> {target_dir.split('/')[-1]}/{new_filename}")
            
    except Exception as e:
        failed_operations.append((old_filename, str(e)))
        print(f"‚úó Failed to process {old_filename}: {e}")

print(f"\nSummary:")
print(f"  Successful operations: {successful_operations}")
print(f"  Failed operations: {len(failed_operations)}")

if len(failed_operations) > 0:
    print(f"  Failed files:")
    for file, error in failed_operations:
        print(f"    {file}: {error}")

# Count files in each directory
c_count = len([f for f in os.listdir(c_path) if f.endswith('.c')])
rust_count = len([f for f in os.listdir(rust_path) if f.endswith('.rs')])
python_count = len([f for f in os.listdir(python_path) if f.endswith('.py')])

print(f"\nFiles organized:")
print(f"  C directory: {c_count} files")
print(f"  Rust directory: {rust_count} files")
print(f"  Python directory: {python_count} files")
print(f"  Total: {c_count + rust_count + python_count} files")
```
</div>

```python 
# Combine all student mappings
student_mapping.update(cs_students)
student_mapping.update(se_students)
student_mapping.update(cs_sec_students)

# Get all code files
workspace_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace"
all_files = []

for file in os.listdir(workspace_path):
    if file.endswith(('.c', '.py', '.rs')) and not file == 'CollegeNameID.xlsx':
        all_files.append(file)

# Patterns to identify Operating Systems Assignment 3 files
os_patterns = [
    r'OperatingSystems.*HW3',
    r'OperatingSystems.*Assignment3',
    r'OperatingSystems.*Lab3',
    r'OS.*Assignment3',
    r'OS.*HW3',
    r'OS.*Homework3',
    r'OS.*Lab3',
    r'OS.*Project3'
]

os_hw3_files = []
for file in all_files:
    for pattern in os_patterns:
        if re.search(pattern, file, re.IGNORECASE):
            os_hw3_files.append(file)
            break

# Filter out non-OS files
os_hw3_files_filtered = []
for file in os_hw3_files:
    # Skip files that are clearly not OS-related
    if any(subject in file for subject in ['Network', 'Database', 'Compiler', 'Algorithm', 'AI', 'SE', 'DS']):
        if not any(os_term in file for os_term in ['OperatingSystems', 'OS']):
            continue
    os_hw3_files_filtered.append(file)

# Create the renaming mapping
rename_operations = []
for file in os_hw3_files_filtered:
    # Extract student name from filename
    name_match = None
    
    # Try different patterns to extract the name
    patterns = [
        r'^([A-Za-z]+ [A-Za-z]+)[-_]',  # "Name Surname-" or "Name Surname_"
        r'^([A-Za-z]+ [A-Za-z]+) ',     # "Name Surname "
    ]
    
    for pattern in patterns:
        match = re.match(pattern, file)
        if match:
            name_match = match.group(1)
            break
    
    if not name_match:
        print(f"Could not extract name from: {file}")
        continue
    
    # Look up student info
    if name_match in student_mapping:
        student_id, college = student_mapping[name_match]
        
        # Get file extension
        extension = file.split('.')[-1]
        
        # Create new filename: Name-College-StudentID-OS-HW3.extension
        new_filename = f"{name_match}-{college}-{student_id}-OS-HW3.{extension}"
        
        rename_operations.append((file, new_filename))
    else:
        print(f"Student not found in mapping: {name_match} (from file: {file})")

print(f"Found {len(os_hw3_files_filtered)} OS HW3 files")
print(f"Successfully mapped {len(rename_operations)} files for renaming")

# Create the os_hw3 directory structure
os_hw3_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace/os_hw3"
c_path = os.path.join(os_hw3_path, "C")
rust_path = os.path.join(os_hw3_path, "Rust")
python_path = os.path.join(os_hw3_path, "Python")

# Create directories
os.makedirs(c_path, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(rust_path, exist_ok=True)
os.makedirs(python_path, exist_ok=True)

print(f"\nCreated directory structure:")
print(f"  {os_hw3_path}/")
print(f"    C/")
print(f"    Rust/")
print(f"    Python/")

# Perform the renaming and moving operations
successful_operations = 0
failed_operations = []

for old_filename, new_filename in rename_operations:
    try:
        old_path = os.path.join(workspace_path, old_filename)
        
        # Determine target directory based on file extension
        extension = new_filename.split('.')[-1].lower()
        if extension == 'c':
            target_dir = c_path
        elif extension == 'rs':
            target_dir = rust_path
        elif extension == 'py':
            target_dir = python_path
        else:
            print(f"Unknown extension: {extension} for file: {new_filename}")
            continue
            
        new_path = os.path.join(target_dir, new_filename)
        
        # Copy and rename the file
        shutil.copy2(old_path, new_path)
        successful_operations += 1
        
        if successful_operations <= 5:  # Show first 5 operations
            print(f"‚úì {old_filename} -> {target_dir.split('/')[-1]}/{new_filename}")
            
    except Exception as e:
        failed_operations.append((old_filename, str(e)))
        print(f"‚úó Failed to process {old_filename}: {e}")

print(f"\nRenaming and organizing completed!")
print(f"  Successful operations: {successful_operations}")
print(f"  Failed operations: {len(failed_operations)}")

# Count files in each directory
c_count = len([f for f in os.listdir(c_path) if f.endswith('.c')])
rust_count = len([f for f in os.listdir(rust_path) if f.endswith('.rs')])
python_count = len([f for f in os.listdir(python_path) if f.endswith('.py')])

print(f"\nFiles organized:")
print(f"  C directory: {c_count} files")
print(f"  Rust directory: {rust_count} files")
print(f"  Python directory: {python_count} files")
print(f"  Total: {c_count + rust_count + python_count} files")
```

```python 
import os

workspace_path = "/workspace/dumps/workspace"

# Get all code files in the main workspace directory
all_code_files = []
for file in os.listdir(workspace_path):
    if file.endswith(('.c', '.py', '.rs')):
        all_code_files.append(file)

print(f"Found {len(all_code_files)} code files to delete from main workspace")

# Delete all code files
deleted_count = 0
failed_deletions = []

for file in all_code_files:
    try:
        file_path = os.path.join(workspace_path, file)
        os.remove(file_path)
        deleted_count += 1
        if deleted_count <= 5:  # Show first 5 deletions
            print(f"‚úì Deleted: {file}")
    except Exception as e:
        failed_deletions.append((file, str(e)))
        print(f"‚úó Failed to delete {file}: {e}")

print(f"\nCleanup completed!")
print(f"  Files deleted: {deleted_count}")
print(f"  Failed deletions: {len(failed_deletions)}")

if len(failed_deletions) > 0:
    print("Failed deletions:")
    for file, error in failed_deletions:
        print(f"  {file}: {error}")

# Verify the workspace is clean
remaining_files = []
for file in os.listdir(workspace_path):
    if file.endswith(('.c', '.py', '.rs')):
        remaining_files.append(file)

if len(remaining_files) == 0:
    print(f"\n‚úì Workspace is now clean - no code files remain in main directory")
else:
    print(f"\n‚ö† Warning: {len(remaining_files)} code files still remain:")
    for file in remaining_files:
        print(f"  {file}")

# Final verification - list what's left in workspace
print(f"\nFinal workspace contents:")
for item in sorted(os.listdir(workspace_path)):
    item_path = os.path.join(workspace_path, item)
    if os.path.isdir(item_path):
        print(f"  [DIR] {item}")
    else:
        print(f"  [FILE] {item}")
```

<svg width="14px" height="14px" viewBox="0 0 32 32" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" style={{margin: 0, padding: 0, display: 'inline-block'}}><path fillRule="evenodd" clipRule="evenodd" d="M13.0164 2C10.8193 2 9.03825 3.72453 9.03825 5.85185V8.51852H15.9235V9.25926H5.97814C3.78107 9.25926 2 10.9838 2 13.1111L2 18.8889C2 21.0162 3.78107 22.7407 5.97814 22.7407H8.27322V19.4815C8.27322 17.3542 10.0543 15.6296 12.2514 15.6296H19.5956C21.4547 15.6296 22.9617 14.1704 22.9617 12.3704V5.85185C22.9617 3.72453 21.1807 2 18.9836 2H13.0164ZM12.0984 6.74074C12.8589 6.74074 13.4754 6.14378 13.4754 5.40741C13.4754 4.67103 12.8589 4.07407 12.0984 4.07407C11.3378 4.07407 10.7213 4.67103 10.7213 5.40741C10.7213 6.14378 11.3378 6.74074 12.0984 6.74074Z" fill="#327EBD"/><path fillRule="evenodd" clipRule="evenodd" d="M18.9834 30C21.1805 30 22.9616 28.2755 22.9616 26.1482V23.4815L16.0763 23.4815L16.0763 22.7408L26.0217 22.7408C28.2188 22.7408 29.9998 21.0162 29.9998 18.8889V13.1111C29.9998 10.9838 28.2188 9.25928 26.0217 9.25928L23.7266 9.25928V12.5185C23.7266 14.6459 21.9455 16.3704 19.7485 16.3704L12.4042 16.3704C10.5451 16.3704 9.03809 17.8296 9.03809 19.6296L9.03809 26.1482C9.03809 28.2755 10.8192 30 13.0162 30H18.9834ZM19.9015 25.2593C19.1409 25.2593 18.5244 25.8562 18.5244 26.5926C18.5244 27.329 19.1409 27.9259 19.9015 27.9259C20.662 27.9259 21.2785 27.329 21.2785 26.5926C21.2785 25.8562 20.662 25.2593 19.9015 25.2593Z" fill="#FFDA4B"/></svg> `python-execute`

```python 

import json
import os

# Load student data from the JSON files
with open("computer_science.json", "r") as f:
    cs_data = json.load(f)

with open("software_engineering.json", "r") as f:
    se_data = json.load(f)

with open("cyber_security.json", "r") as f:
    cy_data = json.load(f)

# Create a unified student database
student_db = {}
for student in cs_data["cells"]:
    if student["column"] == 1 and student["value"]:
        name = student["value"]
        student_db[name] = {
            "id": next((s["value"] for s in cs_data["cells"] if s["row"] == student["row"] and s["column"] == 2), None),
            "college": "Computer Science"
        }

for student in se_data["cells"]:
    if student["column"] == 1 and student["value"]:
        name = student["value"]
        student_db[name] = {
            "id": next((s["value"] for s in se_data["cells"] if s["row"] == student["row"] and s["column"] == 2), None),
            "college": "Software Engineering"
        }

for student in cy_data["cells"]:
    if student["column"] == 1 and student["value"]:
        name = student["value"]
        student_db[name] = {
            "id": next((s["value"] for s in cy_data["cells"] if s["row"] == student["row"] and s["column"] == 2), None),
            "college": "Cyber Security"
        }

# Get the list of all files in the current directory
all_files = os.listdir()

# Iterate over each file
for old_filename in all_files:
    # Check if the file is a potential candidate for renaming
    if any(keyword in old_filename.lower() for keyword in ["os", "operatingsystems", "operating system"]) and \
       any(keyword in old_filename.lower() for keyword in ["hw3", "assignment3", "lab3", "project3"]):
        
        # Extract student name from the filename
        student_name = old_filename.split("-")[0].replace("_", " ")
        
        # Find the student in the database
        if student_name in student_db:
            student_info = student_db[student_name]
            
            # Create the new filename
            new_filename = f\'{student_name}-{student_info["college"]}-{student_info["id"]}-OS-HW3\'{os.path.splitext(old_filename)[1]}'
            
            # Determine the subdirectory based on file extension
            extension = os.path.splitext(old_filename)[1]
            if extension == ".c":
                subdirectory = "C"
            elif extension == ".py":
                subdirectory = "Python"
            elif extension == ".rs":
                subdirectory = "Rust"
            else:
                continue
            
            # Move and rename the file
            os.rename(old_filename, os.path.join("os_hw3", subdirectory, new_filename))

# Get the list of all files again, to delete the remaining ones
all_files = os.listdir()
for filename in all_files:
    if os.path.isfile(filename) and filename not in ["CollegeNameID.xlsx", "computer_science.json", "software_engineering.json", "cyber_security.json"]:
        os.remove(filename)

```
